msg:I stayed here for three days during the May Day holiday.
The hotel room was OK.
Maybe it was because it rained a lot recently and it was close to the sea.
The bed felt a little damp.
The hotel staff were very nice and greeted everyone when they met.
There were many activities in the hotel lobby.
Children could also do small crafts next to the lobby.
The swimming pool was open, but it closed a little early at night (closed at 8pm).
I just came back from dinner and found that it was closed, so I had to swim early in the morning.
The water quality was good, but it was still a little cold in May.
The room included breakfast. There were many types of restaurants.
You could basically eat a lot. There was a small wave pool next door to satisfy the children.
The hotel was very close to the beach, and you could catch crabs and pick up some small shells.
I also saw several jellyfish, but I didnâ€™t dare to touch them because I was afraid they were poisonous.
I always wanted to go to the water world next door, but it was raining. I can only leave a little regret and come again next time.
